â•­â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€ ğŸ¤– Agent Started â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â•®
â”‚                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚  Agent: Documentation Quality Auditor                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚  Task: Given the comparison data from the Code & Documentation Analyzer, score each                                                â”‚
â”‚      file's documentation freshness ,classify severity and confidence.                                                             â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚      YOUR TASKS:                                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚      1.Parse Analyzer Output: Extract all comparison data for each file                                                            â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚      2.Evaluate Scoring Components(assign values 0-1 for each):                                                                    â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚         A. FRESHNESS FACTORS:                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚         - structural_match: Do parameters, return types, and endpoints align?                                                      â”‚
â”‚           * 1.0 = Perfect match                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚           * 0.5 = Some mismatches                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚           * 0.0 = Major structural differences                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚         - semantic_accuracy: Does documentation describe actual behavior?                                                          â”‚
â”‚           * 1.0 = Description perfectly matches implementation                                                                     â”‚
â”‚           * 0.5 = Partially accurate, some outdated info                                                                           â”‚
â”‚           * 0.0 = Description completely wrong                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚         - recency_factor: How recent is the documentation vs code?                                                                 â”‚
â”‚           * 1.0 = Updated within days of code change                                                                               â”‚
â”‚           * 0.5 = Updated within months                                                                                            â”‚
â”‚           * 0.0 = Not updated in 6+ months after code change                                                                       â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚         - completeness: Are all code elements documented?                                                                          â”‚
â”‚           * 1.0 = All functions/classes/methods documented                                                                         â”‚
â”‚           * 0.5 = 50% documented                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚           * 0.0 = Minimal or no documentation                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚         B. CONFIDENCE FACTORS:                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚         - mismatch_clarity: How obvious are the discrepancies?                                                                     â”‚
â”‚           * 1.0 = Clear, objective mismatch (e.g., param count difference)                                                         â”‚
â”‚           * 0.5 = Requires some interpretation                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚           * 0.0 = Highly subjective or unclear                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚         - code_complexity: How complex is the code?                                                                                â”‚
â”‚           * 1.0 = Very complex, hard to understand                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚           * 0.5 = Moderate complexity                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚           * 0.0 = Simple, straightforward                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚         - doc_structure_quality: How well-structured is the documentation?                                                         â”‚
â”‚           * 1.0 = Well-structured, easy to parse                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚           * 0.5 = Acceptable structure                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚           * 0.0 = Poor or no structure                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚      3.Use freshness_scorer Tool: Call the tool with all 7 parameters to get:                                                      â”‚
â”‚         - freshness_score (0-100)                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚         - severity (critical/major/minor)                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚         - confidence (0-1)                                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚         - detailed breakdown                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚      4.Document Specific Issues: For each file, list problems with:                                                                â”‚
â”‚         - Clear description of the issue                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚         - Location (line number or section)                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚         - Expected value (what code shows)                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚         - Actual value (what doc says)                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚         - Impact explanation (why this matters)                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚      5.Provide Recommendations: Actionable steps to improve documentation freshness                                                â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚        SCORING INTERPRETATION:                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚        Freshness Score:                                                                                                            â”‚
â”‚          - < 50% â†’ CRITICAL: Immediate attention required, documentation unusable                                                  â”‚
â”‚          - 50-74% â†’ MAJOR: Should be addressed soon, significant issues                                                            â”‚
â”‚          - >= 75% â†’ MINOR: Low priority, minor improvements needed                                                                 â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚        Confidence Level:                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚          - > 0.8 â†’ HIGH: Very certain about the assessment                                                                         â”‚
â”‚          - 0.5-0.8 â†’ MEDIUM: Reasonably confident                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚          - < 0.5 â†’ LOW: Requires manual review                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚      EXAMPLES:                                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚      Example 1 - Clear Parameter Mismatch:                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚      ```                                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚      freshness_scorer(                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚          structural_match=0.25,      # 1 of 4 params documented                                                                    â”‚
â”‚          semantic_accuracy=0.70,     # Description mostly accurate                                                                 â”‚
â”‚          recency_factor=0.30,        # 6 months outdated                                                                           â”‚
â”‚          completeness=0.60,          # 3 of 5 methods documented                                                                   â”‚
â”‚          mismatch_clarity=0.95,      # Very clear param count difference                                                           â”‚
â”‚          code_complexity=0.40,       # Moderate complexity                                                                         â”‚
â”‚          doc_structure_quality=0.80  # Well-structured docs                                                                        â”‚
â”‚      )                                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚      â†’ Score: ~42% (critical), Confidence: 0.82 (high)                                                                             â”‚
â”‚      ```                                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚      Example 2 - Semantic Drift:                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚      ```                                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚      freshness_scorer(                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚          structural_match=0.90,      # Structure looks good                                                                        â”‚
â”‚          semantic_accuracy=0.40,     # Behavior changed, docs didn't                                                               â”‚
â”‚          recency_factor=0.20,        # Very outdated                                                                               â”‚
â”‚          completeness=0.85,          # Well documented                                                                             â”‚
â”‚          mismatch_clarity=0.45,      # Requires interpretation                                                                     â”‚
â”‚          code_complexity=0.70,       # Complex code                                                                                â”‚
â”‚          doc_structure_quality=0.75  # Good structure                                                                              â”‚
â”‚      )                                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚      â†’ Score: ~61% (major), Confidence: 0.48 (low - needs review)                                                                  â”‚
â”‚      ```                                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚      **OUTPUT REQUIREMENTS:**                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚      Produce a comprehensive JSON report for each file analyzed.                                                                   â”‚

â”‚  arguments, and API specs. Include a traceability matrix in the SRS.                                                               â”‚
â”‚  - **Version Control**: Initialize a Git repository (if not already done) to track changes and tie documentation updates to code   â”‚
â”‚  commits.                                                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚  - **OpenAPI Validation**: Run an OpenAPI validator to confirm `openapi.yaml` matches the FastAPI/Flask routes and update either   â”‚
â”‚  side as needed.                                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚  Addressing these points will eliminate the identified stale documentation, improve developer onboarding, and reduce the risk of   â”‚
â”‚  misuse or bugs caused by undocumented behavior.                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                    â”‚

â•­â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€ ğŸ¤– Agent Started â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â•®
â”‚                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚  Agent: Documentation Quality Auditor                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚  Task: Given the comparison data from the Code & Documentation Analyzer, score each                                                â”‚
â”‚      file's documentation freshness ,classify severity and confidence.                                                             â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚      YOUR TASKS:                                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚      1.Parse Analyzer Output: Extract all comparison data for each file                                                            â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚      2.Evaluate Scoring Components(assign values 0-1 for each):                                                                    â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚         A. FRESHNESS FACTORS:                                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚         - structural_match: Do parameters, return types, and endpoints align?                                                      â”‚
â”‚           * 1.0 = Perfect match                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚           * 0.5 = Some mismatches                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚           * 0.0 = Major structural differences                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚         - semantic_accuracy: Does documentation describe actual behavior?                                                          â”‚
â”‚           * 1.0 = Description perfectly matches implementation                                                                     â”‚
â”‚           * 0.5 = Partially accurate, some outdated info                                                                           â”‚
â”‚           * 0.0 = Description completely wrong                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚         - recency_factor: How recent is the documentation vs code?                                                                 â”‚
â”‚           * 1.0 = Updated within days of code change                                                                               â”‚
â”‚           * 0.5 = Updated within months                                                                                            â”‚
â”‚           * 0.0 = Not updated in 6+ months after code change                                                                       â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚         - completeness: Are all code elements documented?                                                                          â”‚
â”‚           * 1.0 = All functions/classes/methods documented                                                                         â”‚
â”‚           * 0.5 = 50% documented                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚           * 0.0 = Minimal or no documentation                                                                                      â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚         B. CONFIDENCE FACTORS:                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚         - mismatch_clarity: How obvious are the discrepancies?                                                                     â”‚
â”‚           * 1.0 = Clear, objective mismatch (e.g., param count difference)                                                         â”‚
â”‚           * 0.5 = Requires some interpretation                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚           * 0.0 = Highly subjective or unclear                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚         - code_complexity: How complex is the code?                                                                                â”‚
â”‚           * 1.0 = Very complex, hard to understand                                                                                 â”‚
â”‚           * 0.5 = Moderate complexity                                                                                              â”‚
â”‚           * 0.0 = Simple, straightforward                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚         - doc_structure_quality: How well-structured is the documentation?                                                         â”‚
â”‚           * 1.0 = Well-structured, easy to parse                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚           * 0.5 = Acceptable structure                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚           * 0.0 = Poor or no structure                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚      3.Use freshness_scorer Tool: Call the tool with all 7 parameters to get:                                                      â”‚
â”‚         - freshness_score (0-100)                                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚         - severity (critical/major/minor)                                                                                          â”‚
â”‚         - confidence (0-1)                                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚         - detailed breakdown                                                                                                       â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚      4.Document Specific Issues: For each file, list problems with:                                                                â”‚
â”‚         - Clear description of the issue                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚         - Location (line number or section)                                                                                        â”‚
â”‚         - Expected value (what code shows)                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚         - Actual value (what doc says)                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚         - Impact explanation (why this matters)                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚      5.Provide Recommendations: Actionable steps to improve documentation freshness                                                â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚        SCORING INTERPRETATION:                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚        Freshness Score:                                                                                                            â”‚
â”‚          - < 50% â†’ CRITICAL: Immediate attention required, documentation unusable                                                  â”‚
â”‚          - 50-74% â†’ MAJOR: Should be addressed soon, significant issues                                                            â”‚
â”‚          - >= 75% â†’ MINOR: Low priority, minor improvements needed                                                                 â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚        Confidence Level:                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚          - > 0.8 â†’ HIGH: Very certain about the assessment                                                                         â”‚
â”‚          - 0.5-0.8 â†’ MEDIUM: Reasonably confident                                                                                  â”‚
â”‚          - < 0.5 â†’ LOW: Requires manual review                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚      EXAMPLES:                                                                                                                     â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚      Example 1 - Clear Parameter Mismatch:                                                                                         â”‚
â”‚      ```                                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚      freshness_scorer(                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚          structural_match=0.25,      # 1 of 4 params documented                                                                    â”‚
â”‚          semantic_accuracy=0.70,     # Description mostly accurate                                                                 â”‚
â”‚          recency_factor=0.30,        # 6 months outdated                                                                           â”‚
â”‚          completeness=0.60,          # 3 of 5 methods documented                                                                   â”‚
â”‚          mismatch_clarity=0.95,      # Very clear param count difference                                                           â”‚
â”‚          code_complexity=0.40,       # Moderate complexity                                                                         â”‚
â”‚          doc_structure_quality=0.80  # Well-structured docs                                                                        â”‚
â”‚      )                                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚      â†’ Score: ~42% (critical), Confidence: 0.82 (high)                                                                             â”‚
â”‚      ```                                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                    â”‚
â”‚      Example 2 - Semantic Drift:                                                                                                   â”‚
â”‚      ```                                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚      freshness_scorer(                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚          structural_match=0.90,      # Structure looks good                                                                        â”‚
â”‚          semantic_accuracy=0.40,     # Behavior changed, docs didn't                                                               â”‚
â”‚          recency_factor=0.20,        # Very outdated                                                                               â”‚
â”‚          completeness=0.85,          # Well documented                                                                             â”‚
â”‚          mismatch_clarity=0.45,      # Requires interpretation                                                                     â”‚
â”‚          code_complexity=0.70,       # Complex code                                                                                â”‚
â”‚          doc_structure_quality=0.75  # Good structure                                                                              â”‚
â”‚      )                                                                                                                             â”‚
â”‚      â†’ Score: ~61% (major), Confidence: 0.48 (low - needs review)                                                                  â”‚
â”‚      ```                                                                                                                           â”‚
â”‚                                                                                                                                    â”‚

â”‚      Produce a comprehensive JSON report for each file analyzed.                                                                   â”‚
